        (function() {
            function getsec(str) {
                var str1 = str.substring(1, str.length) * 1,
                        str2 = str.substring(0, 1);

                if (str2 == "s") {
                    return str1 * 1000;
                }
                else if (str2 == "h") {
                    return str1 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
                }
                else if (str2 == "d") {
                    return str1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
                }
            }
            function setCookie(name, value, time, path, domain) {
                // setCookie("name","hayden","s20");
                // s20是代表20秒
                // h是指小时，如12小时则是：h12
                // d是天数，30天则：d30

                var strsec = getsec(time);
                var exp = new Date();
                var pathStr = typeof path == 'undefined' ? ";path=/" : ";path="+path;
                var domain = typeof domain == 'undefined' ? "" : ";domain="+domain;

                exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + strsec * 1);
                document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + ";expires=" + exp.toGMTString() + pathStr + domain;
            }
            function getCookie(name) {
                var arr, reg = new RegExp("(^| )" + name + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");

                if (arr = document.cookie.match(reg)){
                    return unescape(decodeURI(arr[2]));
                }else{
                    return null;
                }
            }

            function setABVersion() {
                var bgUser = getCookie('__bguser');
                var abversion = getCookie("abversion");
                if (bgUser) {
                    var abTestNum = bgUser.split('|')[1];
                    abTestNum = abTestNum % 2 ? 1 : 2;
                    if (!abversion || abversion != abTestNum) {
                        setCookie("abversion", abTestNum, 'd365', '/', '.banggood.com');
                    }
                }
            }
            setABVersion();
            window.onBguserSet = function(){
                setABVersion()
            }
        }) ()

		function loadHintSearch() {

				url: homeUrl + 'index.php',
				type : 'get',
				data :'com=index&t=loadHintSearch',
				timeout : 2000,
				dataType:'json',

						$("input[name=keywords]").val(data.tag_name);

						$("input[name=hint_search_tagname]").val(data.tag_name);
						$("input[name=hint_search_url]").val(data.url);
					}
				}
			});
		}

var isloadingGA = false;
$(document).on("click","#pricestorm",function(){
    var val = 0;
    if(typeof(ga) == 'function'){
        isloadingGA = true;
    }
    if($(this).hasClass("checkbox_on_active")){
        if(isloadingGA){
            ga('send', 'event', 'search', 'click', 'top_activitycancel_button_20171101');
        }
        if(typeof(JGData) != 'undefined'){
            JGData.JGCheckClassName(JGData,'top_activitycancel_button_20171101',0,'','17305030325');
        }
    }else{
        if(isloadingGA){
            ga('send', 'event', 'search', 'click', 'top_activity_button_20171101');
        }
        if(typeof(JGData) != 'undefined'){
            JGData.JGCheckClassName(JGData,'top_activity_button_20171101',0,'','17305030352');
        }
        val = $('#price_storm').val();
    }
    doSearch('priceStorm', val);
});

var curPfrom = 0;
var curPto = 0;
var isPriceSel = false;
function searchPrice(form){
    var pfrom = $(form).find('input[name="pfrom"]').val();
    var dpfrom = $(form).find('input[name="pfrom"]').attr('dvalue');
    var pto = $(form).find('input[name="pto"]').val();
    var dpto = $(form).find('input[name="pto"]').attr('dvalue');
    if(pfrom == dpfrom && pto == dpto && pfrom.length > 0 && pto.length > 0){
        return false;
    }
    if(pfrom == '' && pto == ''){
        //return false;
    }
    pfrom = (pfrom == '')?0:pfrom;
    pto = (pto == '')?0:pto;
    curPfrom = pfrom;
    curPto = pto;
    isPriceSel = true;
    doSearch();
    return false;
}

$(document).on("click",".directhouse a",function(){
    if($(this).hasClass("active"))return;
    var houseid = $(this).attr("data-direct-id");
    var text = $(this).text();
    $(this).addClass("active").parent().siblings().find("a").removeClass("active");
    $("#chooseDirect").val(houseid);
    $(this).parents(".directhouse").siblings("a").find("code").text(text);

    doSearch('direct', houseid);
});

function doSearch(key, value) { 
    var urlArr = location.href.split('?');
    var newParams = new Array();
    var params = new Array();
    if (urlArr[1] != undefined) {
        var params = urlArr[1].split('&');
    } 

    var i = 0;
    for (var x =0;x < params.length; x++) {
        var tmp = params[x].split('=');
        if (tmp[0] == 'pfrom' || tmp[0] == 'pto' || tmp[0] == 'currency') {
            continue;
        }
        if (tmp[1] != 0 && tmp[0] != key) { 
            newParams[i] = params[x];
            i++; 
        }
    }
    if (value > 0)
        newParams[i] = key+'='+value;

    var haveCurrency = false;
    //加上价格
    if (curPfrom > 0 || curPto > 0) {
        i++;
        newParams[i] = 'pfrom='+curPfrom;
        i++;
        newParams[i] = 'pto='+curPto;
        haveCurrency = true;
    }else if(!isPriceSel){
        var dvaluePfrom = $('.searchPriceShai').find('input[name="pfrom"]').attr('dvalue');
        curPfrom = (dvaluePfrom != '' && dvaluePfrom != undefined && dvaluePfrom > 0)?parseFloat(dvaluePfrom):0;
        var dvaluePto = $('.searchPriceShai').find('input[name="pto"]').attr('dvalue');
        curPto = (dvaluePto != '' && dvaluePto != undefined && dvaluePto > 0)?parseFloat(dvaluePto):0;
        if(curPfrom > 0 || curPto > 0){
            i++;
            newParams[i] = 'pfrom='+curPfrom;
            i++;
            newParams[i] = 'pto='+curPto;
            haveCurrency = true;
        }
    }else if(isPriceSel && (curPfrom > 0 || curPto > 0)){
        i++;
        newParams[i] = 'pfrom='+curPfrom;
        i++;
        newParams[i] = 'pto='+curPto;
        haveCurrency = true;
    }

    if(productsListCurrency != '' && productsListCurrency != 'USD' && haveCurrency){
        i++;
        newParams[i] = 'currency='+productsListCurrency;
    }

    var curUrl = urlArr[0];
    if (newParams.length > 0) {
        //curUrl = curUrl.replace(/search\/([^\/]*)\/[^\.]*.html/,"search/$1.html");
        //console.log(1,curUrl,3);return;
        newParams.sort();
        curUrl += '?'+newParams.join('&');
    }
    curUrl = curUrl.replace(/-price-\d*-\d*/, "-price-"+ curPfrom +"-"+ curPto);
    curUrl = curUrl.replace(/\?\&/, "?");
    var curUrllen = curUrl.length;
    if (curUrl.substr(curUrllen-1, 1) == '&') {
        curUrl = curUrl.substr(0, curUrllen-1);
    }
    curUrl = curUrl.replace(/_p-\d+/,"_p-1");
    curUrl = curUrl.replace(/_page\d+/,"_page1");
    //console.log(1,curUrl);return;
    window.location.href = curUrl;
}

//如果链接中有direct参数，主动请求
var curWarehouse = 0;
var tmp = location.href.split('direct=');
if (tmp[1] != undefined) {
    tmp = tmp[1].split('&');
    curWarehouse = tmp[0];
}

var warehouseHtml = '';

var productsListWarehouse = {"a0":"All Warehouses","a10":"US Warehouse"};
var storage = 'WyJ1c2EiLCJ1ayIsImF1IiwiZnIiXQ==';
var selectWarehouse = '';
var ajaxStorage = '';

function getProductlistWarehouse() {
    if (ajaxStorage != '') {
        return true;
    }
    ajaxStorage = 1;
    var cateid = $("input[name='cat_id']").val();
    var ajaxUrl = homeUrl + 'load/ajax/getProductlistWarehouse.html';
    var data = 'cateid='+cateid+'&lang='+$.cookie('_bgLang');
    data += '&storage=' + storage;
    if (typeof(queryHandler) != 'undefined') data = queryHandler.attachEncrypt(data);
    $.ajax({
        url: ajaxUrl,
        data: data,
        dataType: 'json',
        success: function(ret) {
            ajaxStorage = productsListWarehouse = ret;
            warehouseHtml = '';
            getWarehouse();
        }
    })
}
/* 67325 */
(function(){
    $(".pageSet .pagesort #top_new_warehouses").hover(function(){
        window.getProductlistWarehouse();
    });
    var oParent = $('.page_filter_options .options_item_brand');
    var brandUl = oParent.find('.pagefilter_brand');
    var brandAli = oParent.find('.pagefilter_brand li');
    var brandMoreBtn = oParent.find('.options_item_btn_more');
    var brandPageBtn = oParent.find('.options_item_btn_page');
    var brandPage = 1;
    //$('.page_filter_options .pagefilter_brand li:gt(29)').hide(); //程序判断，大于30的默认隐藏
    if(brandAli.length>10){
        brandMoreBtn.css('display','inline-block');
    }
    //more
    brandMoreBtn.click(function(){
        brandPageBtn.hide();
        if(!this.onoff){
            //$('.page_filter_options .pagefilter_brand li:lt(30)').show();
            brandUl.css('height','auto');
            $(this).text($(this).attr('data-end'));
            if(brandAli.length>30){
                brandPageBtn.show();
            }
        }else{
            //$('.page_filter_options .pagefilter_brand li:gt(9)').hide();
            brandUl.css('height','42px');
            $(this).text($(this).attr('data-start'));
        }
        //brandToggle();
        this.onoff = !this.onoff;
    });

    //prev
    brandPageBtn.find('.prev').click(function(){
        if($(this).hasClass('nopage'))return;
        if(brandPage<=2){
            $(this).addClass('nopage');
        }
        brandPageBtn.find('.next').removeClass('nopage');
        brandPage--;

        brandMoreBtn.show();

        brandToggle();
    });

    //next
    brandPageBtn.find('.next').click(function(){
        if($(this).hasClass('nopage'))return;
        if(brandPage>=Math.floor(brandAli.length/30)){
            $(this).addClass('nopage');
        }
        brandPageBtn.find('.prev').removeClass('nopage');
        brandPage++;

        if($('.page_filter_options .pagefilter_brand li:gt('+((30*brandPage)-30-1)+')').length<=10){
            brandMoreBtn.hide();
        }else{
            brandMoreBtn.show();
        }

        brandToggle();

    });

    function brandToggle(){
        var brandRows = 30*brandPage;
        brandAli.each(function(){
            var index = $(this).index()+1;
            if(index<=brandRows){
                $(this).show();
            }else{
                $(this).hide();
            }
        });
        $('.page_filter_options .pagefilter_brand li:lt('+(brandRows-30)+')').hide();
    }
})();
/* end 67325 */
</script>

<script>
	var cur_page_com = 'search';

	(function(){
		$('#searchListPageGo').on('click',function(){
			var redirectUrl = $('.page_num').find('a:last').attr('href');
			var totalPage = parseInt($(this).attr('data-page-total'));
			var pageNumTo = parseInt($('.page_go .page_input').val());
			if(cur_page_com == 'search' || cur_page_com == 'wh_search'){
				var preg_word = /_p-\d*/;
				var preg_re_word = '_p-';
			}else if(cur_page_com == 'category' || cur_page_com == 'whcategory'){
                var preg_word = /_page\d*/;
                var preg_re_word = '_page';
			}else{
                var preg_word = /-page\d*/;
                var preg_re_word = '-page';
			}
			if (pageNumTo > totalPage) {
				var burUrl = redirectUrl.replace(preg_word, preg_re_word+ totalPage);
				window.location.href=burUrl;
				//return false;
			}else if(pageNumTo > 0){
				var curUrl = redirectUrl.replace(preg_word, preg_re_word+ pageNumTo);
				window.location.href=curUrl;
				//return false;
			}
		});
	})();

</script>

	<div class="clear"></div>
				
						<script type="text/javascript">
				var cateId = '0';
				var keywords = 't shirt';
                var pids = '1452748,1457432,1451441,1451439,1461247,1451440,1411785,1456556,1066275,1348931,1282748,1465613,1339992,1465773,1451065,1420448,1322645,1361733,1431073,1283383,1449206,1458275,1442252,1444078,1457431,1463617,1470722,1453779,1360424,1470721,1461105,1456555,1447022,1439022,1331791,1336716,1434872,1342406,1455385,1381755,1457797,1311958,1451062,1265134,';
				var lang = 'en-GB';
				var pidNum = 44;
				
				function productNameHighLight(keywords){
					if(typeof(keywords) == 'undefined' || keywords.length == 0){
						return false;
					}
					var arr = keywords.split(/\s/);
					$('.goodlist_1 .title a').each(function(){
						var text = $(this).text();
						for(var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++){
							var word = arr[i];
							var matchWord = word.match(/[\,\&\'\~\"\*\%\/\$\^\!\|\(\)\.\-\s]*(.*)[\,\&\'\~\"\*\%\/\$\^\!\|\(\)\.\-\s]*/);
							word = matchWord[1].replace(/[\,\&\'\~\"\*\%\/\$\^\!\|\(\)\-\s]/g," ");
							if(word == '' || word == ' ')continue;
							if(word != 'b'){
								word = word.replace('\.','\\\.');
								word = word.replace('\+','\\\+');
								//console.log(word,1);
								//var regexp = new RegExp("\\b("+word+")\\b", "ig");
								//console.log(text,2);
								if(lang == 'jp-JP'){
									var regexp = new RegExp("("+word+")", "ig");
								}else{
									var regexp = new RegExp("\\b("+word+")\\b", "ig");
								}
								text = text.replace(eval(regexp), "<b>$1</b>");
								//console.log(text,3);
							} else {
								var regexp = new RegExp("[^<](b)[^>]", "ig");
								text = text.replace(regexp, "<b>b</b>");
							}
						}
						$(this).html(text);
					});
				}
				productNameHighLight(keywords);
				/*$(function(){
					productNameHighLight(keywords);
				});*/
				$("#clickMore").on("click",function(){
					$(".hide").show();
					$("#clickMore").hide();
					$("#clickLess").show();
				});
				$("#clickLess").on("click",function(){
					$(".hide").hide();
					$("#clickMore").show();
					$("#clickLess").hide();
				});
                function recordKeyword(keywords, pids){
                    if(typeof(keywords) == 'undefined' || keywords.length == 0){
                        return;
                    }
                    if(pidNum > 0){
                        var getMaybe = 0;
					}else{
                        var getMaybe = 1;
					}
                    $.ajax({
                        url: homeUrl + 'index.php',
                        type: 'get',
	                    data: {'com': 'ajax', 't': 'recordSearch', 'keywords': keywords, 'pids': pids, 'type': 2,'getMaybe':getMaybe},
	                    success : function(res){
							if (res) {
								$('.listlookingfor .goodlist_1').replaceWith(res);
							}
	                    },
                    })
                }
                recordKeyword(keywords, pids);

                function RecHotproduct(){
					var lang = $.cookie("_bgLang");
					var url = homeUrl + 'searchLeftSide-'+keywords+'-'+cateId+'.html?x='+parseInt(10*Math.random())+'&lang='+lang;
					$.ajax({
						url:url,
						timeout : 10000,
						type : 'get',
						dataType:'html',
						success:function(html){
							$('.wrap_left').append(html);
							$('.hotlist_2').addClass('rec_purchases');
						}
					});
				}
				setTimeout("RecHotproduct()",1500);
				
			</script>

		</div>
	</div>

		<script>
			function SubmitandSearch(obj){
				var o = $(obj);
				var textarea = o.parent().find('textarea');
				var val = modificationTxt(textarea.val());
				if(!val){
					textarea.focus();
					return false;
				}else{
					var value = val.split(' ');
					if(value.length>1){
						val = value.join('-')
					}
					//$('.nav_category .submit').trigger("click");

					o.parent().slideUp(300);
                    sendsearchAjax(3);
                    window.location.href= '/search/'+val+'.html?sc=1';
				}
			}

			function sendsearchAjax(source){
				$.ajax({
                    url: homeUrl + 'index.php',
                    type: 'get',
                    data: {'com': 'ajax', 't': 'insertCorrect', 'keywords': keywords, 'correct': $('textarea[name="modification"]').val(),'source':source,'forceKeyword':forceKeyword},
                    success : function(){
                    }
                });
			}

			$(document).on('click','.errorcorrection_item .edit_icon',function(){
				if($(this).hasClass('active')){
					$('.suggestmodificationbox').slideUp(300);
					$(this).removeClass('active');
				}else{
					$('.suggestmodificationbox').slideDown(300);
					$(this).addClass('active');
				}
				sendsearchAjax(1);
			});
			$(document).on('click','.suggestmodificationbox .cancel,.suggestmodificationbox .suggest_remove',function(){
				$('.suggestmodificationbox').slideUp(300);
				$('.errorcorrection_item .edit_icon').removeClass('active');
				if($(this).hasClass('suggest_remove')){
					sendsearchAjax(2);
                }
			});

			$(document).click(function(event){
				if($(event.target).parents(".errorcorrection_item").length == 0)
				{
					$('.suggestmodificationbox').slideUp(300);
					$('.errorcorrection_item .edit_icon').removeClass('active');
				}
			});
			function modificationTxt(str) {
	            var RexStr = /\<|\>|\"|\'|\~|\!|\#|\@|\$|\%|\^|\*|\(|\)|\=|\-|\.|\:|\,|\[|\]|\{|\}|\;|\/|\||\\|\?|\&/g;
	            str = str.replace(RexStr, function(MatchStr) {
	                switch (MatchStr) {
	                case "<":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case ">":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "\\":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "/":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "|":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "'":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "&":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "~":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "!":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "@":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "#":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "$":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "%":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "^":
	                    return " ";break;
	               	case "*":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "(":
	                    return " ";break;
	               	case ")":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "-":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "+":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case ":":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case ".":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case ",":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "=":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "[":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "]":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "{":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "}":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case ";":
	                    return " ";break;
	                case "?":
	                    return " ";break;
	                default:
	                    break;
	                };
	            });
	            return str;
	        }
		</script>
